 2762  complexes. Beyond structural information, NMR offers insights into the complexes’ electronic structure,
 2763  since there is a direct relationship between the NMR chemical shift and the frontier molecular orbitals.1 The
 2764  Group-4 metallocenes with bis-h5 cyclopentadienyl ligands are important examples of catalysts used in
 2765  olefin insertion process.2-4 Studying the behavior of the shielding effects in these complexes is of relevance
 2766  to understand their reactivity.

 3409  scp beto93@saga.sigma2.no:Nuclear Magnetic Resonance (NMR) is an important technique for the characterization of transition-metal
 3410  complexes. Beyond structural information, NMR offers insights into the complexes’ electronic structure,
 3411  since there is a direct relationship between the NMR chemical shift and the frontier molecular orbitals.1 The
 3412  Group-4 metallocenes with bis-h5 cyclopentadienyl ligands are important examples of catalysts used in
 3413  olefin insertion process.2-4 Studying the behavior of the shielding effects in these complexes is of relevance
 3414  to understand their reactivity.
 3415  In this combined experimental and computational study, we analyzed the 19F NMR signatures of Cp2MF2,
 3416  Cp*2MF2, and rac-(ebthi)MF2 (M = Ti, Zr, and Hf) metallocene difluorides. The aim is to understand the
 3417  chemical shift changes observed in the solution and solid-state 19F NMR spectra of these complexes. It is of
 3418  interest to explain what is the effect of the metal centre and the Cp, Cp*, and rac-(ebthi) ligands on the 19F
 3419  NMR chemical shift. In particular, we used the Natural Chemical Shift (NCS)5 analysis to understand the

 3660  olefin insertion process.2-4 Studying the behavior of the shielding effects in these complexes is of relevance
 3661  to understand their reactivity.
 3662  In this combined experimental and computational study, we analyzed the 19F NMR signatures of Cp2MF2,
 3663  Cp*2MF2, and rac-(ebthi)MF2 (M = Ti, Zr, and Hf) metallocene difluorides. The aim is to understand the
 3664  chemical shift changes observed in the solution and solid-state 19F NMR spectra of these complexes. It is of
 3665  interest to explain what is the effect of the metal centre and the Cp, Cp*, and rac-(ebthi) ligands on the 19F
 3666  NMR chemical shift. In particular, we used the Natural Chemical Shift (NCS)5 analysis to understand the
